## Idea

Any two maps `f : A → B` and `g : C → D` induce a map
`map-coproduct f g : coproduct A B → coproduct C D`.

## Definitions

### The functorial action of the coproduct operation

<pre class="Agda"><a id="1851" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="1858" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1858" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="1862" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1863" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1863" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="1866" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1866" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="1869" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1869" class="Bound">l1&#39;</a> <a id="1873" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1873" class="Bound">l2&#39;</a> <a id="1877" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1879" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="1884" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1886" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1887" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1887" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1889" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1891" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="1894" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1863" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="1896" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1898" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1899" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1899" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="1901" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1903" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="1906" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1866" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="1908" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1910" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1911" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1911" class="Bound">A&#39;</a> <a id="1914" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1916" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="1919" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1869" class="Bound">l1&#39;</a><a id="1922" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1924" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1925" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1925" class="Bound">B&#39;</a> <a id="1928" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1930" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="1933" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1873" class="Bound">l2&#39;</a><a id="1936" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="1940" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="1949" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1949" class="Function">map-coproduct</a> <a id="1963" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1966" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1887" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1968" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1970" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1911" class="Bound">A&#39;</a><a id="1972" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1974" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1976" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1977" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1899" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="1979" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1981" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1925" class="Bound">B&#39;</a><a id="1983" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1985" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1987" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1887" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1989" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#389" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="1991" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1899" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="1993" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1995" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1911" class="Bound">A&#39;</a> <a id="1998" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#389" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="2000" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1925" class="Bound">B&#39;</a>

## Properties

### Functoriality of coproducts preserves identity maps

<pre class="Agda"><a id="2168" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="2175" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2175" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="2179" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2180" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2180" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="2183" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2183" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="2186" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2188" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="2193" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2195" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2196" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2196" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2198" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2200" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2203" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2180" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="2205" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2207" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2208" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2208" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2210" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2212" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2215" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2183" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="2217" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="2221" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="2230" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2230" class="Function">id-map-coproduct</a> <a id="2247" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2249" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2250" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1949" class="Function">map-coproduct</a> <a id="2264" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2265" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#307" class="Function">id</a> <a id="2268" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2269" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="2271" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2273" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2196" class="Bound">A</a><a id="2274" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="2277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2278" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#307" class="Function">id</a> <a id="2281" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2282" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="2284" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2286" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2208" class="Bound">B</a><a id="2287" class="Symbol">}))</a> <a id="2291" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="2293" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#307" class="Function">id</a>

### Functoriality of coproducts preserves composition

<pre class="Agda"><a id="2432" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="2439" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2439" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="2443" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2444" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2444" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="2447" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2447" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="2450" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2450" class="Bound">l1&#39;</a> <a id="2454" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2454" class="Bound">l2&#39;</a> <a id="2458" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2458" class="Bound">l1&#39;&#39;</a> <a id="2463" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2463" class="Bound">l2&#39;&#39;</a> <a id="2468" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2470" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="2475" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="2479" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2480" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2480" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2482" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2484" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2487" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2444" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="2489" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2491" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2492" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2492" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2494" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2496" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2499" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2447" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="2501" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2503" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2504" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2504" class="Bound">A&#39;</a> <a id="2507" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2509" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2512" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2450" class="Bound">l1&#39;</a><a id="2515" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2517" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2518" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2518" class="Bound">B&#39;</a> <a id="2521" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2523" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2526" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2454" class="Bound">l2&#39;</a><a id="2529" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="2533" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2534" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2534" class="Bound">A&#39;&#39;</a> <a id="2538" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2540" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2543" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2458" class="Bound">l1&#39;&#39;</a><a id="2547" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2549" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2550" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2550" class="Bound">B&#39;&#39;</a> <a id="2554" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2556" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="2559" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2463" class="Bound">l2&#39;&#39;</a><a id="2563" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="2567" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2568" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2568" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2570" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2572" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2480" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2574" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2576" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2504" class="Bound">A&#39;</a><a id="2578" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2580" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2581" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2581" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="2584" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2586" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2504" class="Bound">A&#39;</a> <a id="2589" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2591" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2534" class="Bound">A&#39;&#39;</a><a id="2594" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2596" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2597" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2597" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="2599" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2601" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2492" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2603" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2605" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2518" class="Bound">B&#39;</a><a id="2607" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2610" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2610" class="Bound">g&#39;</a> <a id="2613" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2615" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2518" class="Bound">B&#39;</a> <a id="2618" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2620" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2550" class="Bound">B&#39;&#39;</a><a id="2623" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="2627" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="2636" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2636" class="Function">preserves-comp-map-coproduct</a> <a id="2665" class="Symbol">:</a>

      <a id="9796" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9798" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#9437" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="9800" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#9444" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9802" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#9452" class="Bound">y</a><a id="9803" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Functoriality of coproducts preserves surjections

<pre class="Agda"><a id="9873" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="9880" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#9880" class="Module">_</a>

### For any two maps `f : A → B` and `g : C → D`, there is at most one pair of maps `f' : A → B` and `g' : C → D` such that `f' + g' = f + g`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-contr-fiber-map-coproduct"></a><a id="10709" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#10709" class="Function">is-contr-fiber-map-coproduct</a> <a id="10738" class="Symbol">:</a>

        <a id="11193" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11195" href="foundation.functoriality-cartesian-product-types.html#4271" class="Function">equiv-product</a>
          <a id="11219" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11221" href="foundation-core.functoriality-dependent-function-types.html#2506" class="Function">equiv-Π-equiv-family</a>
            <a id="11254" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11256" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="11258" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11258" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="11260" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11262" href="foundation.equality-coproduct-types.html#4526" class="Function">compute-eq-coproduct-inl-inl</a> <a id="11291" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11292" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#681" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="11296" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11179" class="Bound">fg&#39;</a> <a id="11300" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11258" class="Bound">a</a><a id="11301" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11303" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11304" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11013" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11306" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11258" class="Bound">a</a><a id="11307" class="Symbol">)))</a>
          <a id="11321" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11323" href="foundation-core.functoriality-dependent-function-types.html#2506" class="Function">equiv-Π-equiv-family</a>
            <a id="11356" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11358" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="11360" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11360" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="11362" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11364" href="foundation.equality-coproduct-types.html#7975" class="Function">compute-eq-coproduct-inr-inr</a> <a id="11393" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11394" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#693" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="11398" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11179" class="Bound">fg&#39;</a> <a id="11402" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11360" class="Bound">c</a><a id="11403" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11405" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11406" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11015" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11408" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11360" class="Bound">c</a><a id="11409" class="Symbol">))))</a> <a id="11414" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#13323" class="Function Operator">∘e</a>
        <a id="11425" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11427" href="foundation.universal-property-coproduct-types.html#1489" class="Function">equiv-dependent-universal-property-coproduct</a>
          <a id="11482" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11484" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="11486" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11486" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="11488" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11490" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1949" class="Function">map-coproduct</a> <a id="11504" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11505" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#681" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="11509" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11179" class="Bound">fg&#39;</a><a id="11512" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11514" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11515" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#693" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="11519" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11179" class="Bound">fg&#39;</a><a id="11522" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11524" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11486" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="11526" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2713" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="11528" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1949" class="Function">map-coproduct</a> <a id="11542" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11013" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11544" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11015" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11546" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11486" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11547" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="11550" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#13323" class="Function Operator">∘e</a>
        <a id="11561" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11563" href="foundation.function-extensionality.html#4394" class="Function">equiv-funext</a><a id="11575" class="Symbol">)))</a>
    <a id="11583" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11585" href="foundation.structure-identity-principle.html#1046" class="Function">is-torsorial-Eq-structure</a>
      <a id="11617" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11619" href="foundation.homotopy-induction.html#2866" class="Function">is-torsorial-htpy&#39;</a> <a id="11638" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11013" class="Bound">f</a><a id="11639" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="11647" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11649" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11013" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11651" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#787" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11653" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2724" class="Function">refl-htpy</a><a id="11662" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="11670" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11672" href="foundation.homotopy-induction.html#2866" class="Function">is-torsorial-htpy&#39;</a> <a id="11691" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11015" class="Bound">g</a><a id="11692" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### For any equivalence `f : A + B ≃ A + B` and `g : B ≃ B` such that `f` and `g` coincide on `B`, we construct an `h : A ≃ A` such that `htpy-equiv (equiv-coproduct h d) f`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="11883" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="11890" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11890" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="11894" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11895" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11895" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="11898" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11898" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="11901" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11903" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="11908" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11910" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11911" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11911" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11913" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11915" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="11918" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11895" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="11920" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11922" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11923" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11923" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="11925" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11927" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="11930" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11898" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="11932" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="11936" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="11945" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#11945" class="Function">equiv-coproduct-induce-equiv-disjoint</a> <a id="11983" class="Symbol">:</a>

    <a id="17204" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17011" class="Function">commutative-square-inl-retraction-equiv-coproduct</a> <a id="17254" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17254" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17256" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17257" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#458" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="17261" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17261" class="Bound">y</a><a id="17262" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17264" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17264" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="17266" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17268" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17264" class="Bound">q</a>
    <a id="17274" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17011" class="Function">commutative-square-inl-retraction-equiv-coproduct</a> <a id="17324" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17324" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17326" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17327" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#476" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="17331" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17331" class="Bound">y</a><a id="17332" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17334" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17334" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="17336" class="Symbol">=</a>

  <a id="17407" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#693" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="17411" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17412" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#15695" class="Function">retraction-equiv-coproduct</a> <a id="17439" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17439" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="17441" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17441" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="17443" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17443" class="Bound">p</a><a id="17444" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17446" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17447" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#476" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="17451" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17451" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17452" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17454" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17456" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17443" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="17458" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17451" class="Bound">x</a>
</pre>
### Equivalences between mutually exclusive coproducts

If `P → ¬ Q'` and `P' → ¬ Q` then `(P + Q ≃ P' + Q') ≃ ((P ≃ P') × (Q ≃ Q'))`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="17609" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="17616" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17616" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="17620" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17621" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17621" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="17624" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17624" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="17627" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17627" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="17630" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17630" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="17633" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17635" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="17640" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="17644" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17645" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17645" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="17647" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17649" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="17652" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17621" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="17654" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17656" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17657" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17657" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="17659" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17661" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="17664" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17624" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="17666" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17668" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17669" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17669" class="Bound">P&#39;</a> <a id="17672" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17674" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="17677" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17627" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="17679" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17681" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17682" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17682" class="Bound">Q&#39;</a> <a id="17685" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17687" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="17690" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17630" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="17692" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="17696" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17697" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17697" class="Bound">¬PQ&#39;</a> <a id="17702" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17704" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17645" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="17706" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17708" href="foundation-core.negation.html#595" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="17710" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17682" class="Bound">Q&#39;</a><a id="17712" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="17716" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="17725" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17725" class="Function">left-to-left</a> <a id="17738" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="17744" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17745" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17745" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="17747" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17749" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17750" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17645" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="17752" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#389" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="17754" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17657" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="17755" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17757" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2554" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="17759" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17760" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17669" class="Bound">P&#39;</a> <a id="17763" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#389" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="17765" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17682" class="Bound">Q&#39;</a><a id="17767" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="17770" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="17776" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17777" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17777" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="17779" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17781" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17645" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="17783" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#389" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="17785" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17657" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="17786" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17788" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17790" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1102" class="Function">is-left</a> <a id="17798" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17777" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="17800" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17802" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1102" class="Function">is-left</a> <a id="17810" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17811" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2754" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="17821" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17745" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="17823" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17777" class="Bound">u</a><a id="17824" class="Symbol">)</a>

              <a id="20548" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20550" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2754" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="20560" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20388" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20562" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20563" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#458" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="20567" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20442" class="Bound">p</a><a id="20568" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20570" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#787" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20572" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#17725" class="Function">left-to-left</a> <a id="20585" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18414" class="Bound">¬PQ&#39;</a> <a id="20590" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20388" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20592" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20593" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#458" class="InductiveConstructor">inl</a> <a id="20597" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20442" class="Bound">p</a><a id="20598" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20600" href="foundation.unit-type.html#857" class="InductiveConstructor">star</a><a id="20604" class="Symbol">))</a>
        <a id="20615" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20617" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#476" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="20621" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20621" class="Bound">q</a><a id="20622" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20624" class="Symbol">→</a>
          <a id="20636" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a>
            <a id="20651" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20653" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#681" class="Field">pr1</a><a id="20656" class="Symbol">)</a>
            <a id="20670" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20672" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#4550" class="Function">is-retraction-map-inv-equiv-right-summand</a>
              <a id="20728" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20730" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2754" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="20740" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20388" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20742" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20743" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#476" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="20747" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20621" class="Bound">q</a><a id="20748" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20750" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#787" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20752" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18080" class="Function">right-to-right</a> <a id="20767" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18432" class="Bound">¬P&#39;Q</a> <a id="20772" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20388" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20774" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20775" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#476" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="20779" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20621" class="Bound">q</a><a id="20780" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20782" href="foundation.unit-type.html#857" class="InductiveConstructor">star</a><a id="20786" class="Symbol">)))</a>

  <a id="20793" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20793" class="Function">equiv-mutually-exclusive-coproduct</a> <a id="20828" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="20834" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="20836" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18362" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="20838" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#389" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="20840" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18374" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="20841" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20843" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2554" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="20845" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20846" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18386" class="Bound">P&#39;</a> <a id="20849" href="foundation-core.coproduct-types.html#389" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="20851" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18399" class="Bound">Q&#39;</a><a id="20853" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="20856" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2554" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="20858" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="20860" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18362" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="20862" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2554" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="20864" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18386" class="Bound">P&#39;</a><a id="20866" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20868" href="foundation-core.cartesian-product-types.html#585" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="20870" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20871" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18374" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="20873" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#2554" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="20875" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#18399" class="Bound">Q&#39;</a><a id="20877" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="20882" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#681" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="20886" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20793" class="Function">equiv-mutually-exclusive-coproduct</a> <a id="20921" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20923" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#19351" class="Function">map-mutually-exclusive-coproduct</a>
  <a id="20958" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#693" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="20962" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20793" class="Function">equiv-mutually-exclusive-coproduct</a> <a id="20997" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="21003" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#4851" class="Function">is-equiv-is-invertible</a>
      <a id="21032" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#19739" class="Function">map-inv-mutually-exclusive-coproduct</a>
      <a id="21075" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#19900" class="Function">is-retraction-map-inv-mutually-exclusive-coproduct</a>
      <a id="21132" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#20197" class="Function">is-section-map-inv-mutually-exclusive-coproduct</a>
</pre>
### The functorial action of coproducts on arrows

Given a pair of [morphisms of arrows](foundation.morphisms-arrows.md)
`α : f → g` and `β : h → i`, there is an induced morphism of arrows
`α + β : f + h → g + i` and this construction is functorial.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="21444" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="21451" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21451" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="21455" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21456" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21456" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="21459" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21459" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="21462" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21462" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="21465" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21465" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="21468" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21468" class="Bound">l5</a> <a id="21471" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21471" class="Bound">l6</a> <a id="21474" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21474" class="Bound">l7</a> <a id="21477" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21477" class="Bound">l8</a> <a id="21480" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21482" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="21487" class="Symbol">}</a>

        <a id="22349" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22351" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21616" class="Bound">h</a><a id="22352" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="22362" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22364" href="foundation.morphisms-arrows.html#1826" class="Function">map-codomain-hom-arrow</a> <a id="22387" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21616" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="22389" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21628" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="22391" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21662" class="Bound">β</a><a id="22392" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="22396" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#3099" class="Function Operator">∙h</a>
    <a id="22403" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22405" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#3062" class="Function">htpy-map-coproduct</a> <a id="22424" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22425" href="foundation.morphisms-arrows.html#1909" class="Function">coh-hom-arrow</a> <a id="22439" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21592" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="22441" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21604" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="22443" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21642" class="Bound">α</a><a id="22444" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22446" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22447" href="foundation.morphisms-arrows.html#1909" class="Function">coh-hom-arrow</a> <a id="22461" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21616" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="22463" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21628" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="22465" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21662" class="Bound">β</a><a id="22466" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="22469" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#3099" class="Function Operator">∙h</a>
    <a id="22476" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22478" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#2636" class="Function">preserves-comp-map-coproduct</a>
      <a id="22513" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22515" href="foundation.morphisms-arrows.html#1753" class="Function">map-domain-hom-arrow</a> <a id="22536" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21592" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="22538" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21604" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="22540" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21642" class="Bound">α</a><a id="22541" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22543" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21604" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="22545" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22546" href="foundation.morphisms-arrows.html#1753" class="Function">map-domain-hom-arrow</a> <a id="22567" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21616" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="22569" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21628" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="22571" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21662" class="Bound">β</a><a id="22572" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22574" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21628" class="Bound">i</a><a id="22575" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="22580" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#22580" class="Function">coproduct-hom-arrow</a> <a id="22600" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22602" href="foundation.morphisms-arrows.html#1649" class="Function">hom-arrow</a> <a id="22612" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22613" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1949" class="Function">map-coproduct</a> <a id="22627" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21592" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="22629" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21616" class="Bound">h</a><a id="22630" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22633" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#1949" class="Function">map-coproduct</a> <a id="22647" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21604" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="22649" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21628" class="Bound">i</a><a id="22650" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="22654" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#22580" class="Function">coproduct-hom-arrow</a> <a id="22674" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="22680" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22682" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21692" class="Function">map-domain-coproduct-hom-arrow</a> <a id="22713" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#787" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a>
      <a id="22721" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#21853" class="Function">map-codomain-coproduct-hom-arrow</a> <a id="22754" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#787" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a>
      <a id="22762" href="foundation.functoriality-coproduct-types.html#22022" class="Function">coh-coproduct-hom-arrow</a><a id="22785" class="Symbol">)</a>

  [`foundation.type-arithmetic-coproduct-types`](foundation.type-arithmetic-coproduct-types.md).
- Equality proofs in coproduct types are characterized in
  [`foundation.equality-coproduct-types`](foundation.equality-coproduct-types.md).
- The universal property of coproducts is treated in
  [`foundation.universal-property-coproduct-types`](foundation.universal-property-coproduct-types.md).
- Functorial properties of cartesian product types are recorded in
  [`foundation.functoriality-cartesian-product-types`](foundation.functoriality-cartesian-product-types.md).
- Functorial properties of dependent pair types are recorded in
  [`foundation.functoriality-dependent-pair-types`](foundation.functoriality-dependent-pair-types.md).
